A Transformer is a model architecture that uses self-attention mechanisms to process sequential input data by capturing context from all positions in the sequence, regardless of distance. Self-attention allows the model to weigh the importance of different words in the input when generating an output for a specific word. The mechanism calculates scores (dot products) between query, key, and value vectors derived from input embeddings. These scores determine how much attention each word should pay to others in the sequence.\\n\\nKey formula in self-attention: Attention(Q, K, V) = softmax((Q * K^T) / sqrt(d_k)) * V\\n\\nHere, Q, K, V are the query, key, and value matrices, and d_k is the dimension of the key vectors.\\n\\nHands-on task #1:\\n- Implement a basic self-attention mechanism in PyTorch or TensorFlow.\\n- Use a simple text sequence (e.g., a sentence) as input. The model infers what is required.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Prompt Engineering:\\nPrompt engineering fine-tunes the model’s behavior through careful design of the input prompt. This ensures the model understands the task effectively.\\n\\n#### Strategies:\\n1. **Instructional Prompts**:\\n   - Be explicit about the task: \\"Classify the sentiment as positive, negative, or neutral: \'I love the product.\'\\"\\n\\n2. **Chain-of-Thought Prompting**:\\n   - Guide the model step-by-step: \\"Solve the following logic problem by breaking it into smaller steps...\\"\\n\\n3. **Contextual Information**:\\n   - Provide relevant context, for example: \\"Based on the following patient symptoms, infer the most likely diagnosis.\\"\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Exercise Task #5: \\nUse GPT-3 for Few-Shot Learning and Prompt Engineering:\\n1.
